#### What type of PR is this?
/kind feature
/kind api-change

#### What this PR does / why we need it:
Part of the KEP#168-2

#### Which issue(s) this PR fixes:
Part of #168 

#### Special notes for your reviewer:
In order to test it, create pending workloads and then send requests:
``` kubectl get --raw /apis/visibility.kueue.x-k8s.io/v1alpha1/clusterqueues/<CQ-NAME>/pendingworkloads```

#### Does this PR introduce a user-facing change?
```release-note
Visibility API: Introduce an on-demand API endpoint for fetching pending workloads in a ClusterQueue.
```

### Comment by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-11-22T14:51:21Z

This failure looks related: "https://prow.k8s.io/view/gs/kubernetes-jenkins/pr-logs/pull/kubernetes-sigs_kueue/1251/pull-kueue-test-e2e-main-1-26/1727335355239108608". I suspect this is the issue with the mechanism to evict the sampleJob1.

Then, we can have a follow up issue to improve execution time of the e2e tests more holistically.

```diff
+
+// User-facing representation of a PendingWorkload in ClusterQueue that summarizes neccessary information from the admission order perspective
+type PendingWorkloadSummary struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta   `json:",inline"`
+	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
+
+	LocalQueueName         string `json:"localQueueName,omitempty"`
+	PositionInClusterQueue int32  `json:"positionInClusterQueue,omitempty"`
+	PositionInLocalQueue   int32  `json:"positionInLocalQueue,omitempty"`
+	Priority               int32  `json:"priority,omitempty"`
+}
+

+// +k8s:openapi-gen=true
+
+// PendingWorkloadSummaryList contains a list of ResourceClaim
```

  ```suggestion
  // PendingWorkloadSummaryList contains a list of pending workloads in the context
  // of the query (within LocalQueue or ClusterQueue).
  ```

- **pkg/visibility/config.go:43** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-10-26T14:38:32Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,64 @@
+// Copyright 2023 The Kubernetes Authors.
+//
+// Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+// you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+// You may obtain a copy of the License at
+//
+//	http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
+//
+// Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+// distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+// WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+// See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+// limitations under the License.
+package visibility
+
+import (
+	"strings"
+
+	openapinamer "k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/openapi"
+	genericapiserver "k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server"
+	"k8s.io/client-go/pkg/version"
+	_ "k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/restclient" // for client-go metrics registration
+
+	generatedopenapi "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/api_extension/v1alpha1/openapi"
+
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/queue"
+
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/visibility/api"
+)
+
+type Config struct {
+	Apiserver *genericapiserver.Config
+}
+
+func NewVisibilityServerConfig(recommendedConfig *genericapiserver.RecommendedConfig) *Config {
+	versionGet := version.Get()
+	recommendedConfig.Config.Version = &versionGet
+	// enable OpenAPI schemas
+	recommendedConfig.Config.OpenAPIConfig = genericapiserver.DefaultOpenAPIConfig(generatedopenapi.GetOpenAPIDefinitions, openapinamer.NewDefinitionNamer(api.Scheme))
+	recommendedConfig.Config.OpenAPIV3Config = genericapiserver.DefaultOpenAPIV3Config(generatedopenapi.GetOpenAPIDefinitions, openapinamer.NewDefinitionNamer(api.Scheme))
+	recommendedConfig.Config.OpenAPIConfig.Info.Title = "Kueue visibility-server"
+	recommendedConfig.Config.OpenAPIV3Config.Info.Title = "Kueue visibility-server"
+	recommendedConfig.Config.OpenAPIConfig.Info.Version = strings.Split(recommendedConfig.Config.Version.String(), "-")[0] // TODO(directxman12): remove this once autosetting this doesn't require security definitions
```

  ```suggestion
  	recommendedConfig.Config.OpenAPIConfig.Info.Version = strings.Split(recommendedConfig.Config.Version.String(), "-")[0]
  ```

```diff
+package api

+

+	metainternalversion "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/internalversion"

+)
+
+type pendingWorkloadsInCQ struct {
+	kueueMgr *queue.Manager
+	log      logr.Logger
+}
+
+const (
+	WholeSnapshot = 100000
+)
+
+var _ rest.KindProvider = &pendingWorkloadsInCQ{}
+var _ rest.Storage = &pendingWorkloadsInCQ{}
+var _ rest.Getter = &pendingWorkloadsInCQ{}
+var _ rest.Lister = &pendingWorkloadsInCQ{}
+var _ rest.Scoper = &pendingWorkloadsInCQ{}
+var _ rest.TableConvertor = &pendingWorkloadsInCQ{}
+var _ rest.SingularNameProvider = &pendingWorkloadsInCQ{}
+
+func newPendingWorkloadsInCQ(kueueMgr *queue.Manager) *pendingWorkloadsInCQ {
+	return &pendingWorkloadsInCQ{
+		kueueMgr: kueueMgr,
+		log:      ctrl.Log.WithName("pending-workload-cq"),
+	}
+}
+
+// New implements rest.Storage interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCQ) New() runtime.Object {
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummary{}
+}
+
+// Destroy implements rest.Storage interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCQ) Destroy() {
+}
+
+// Kind implements rest.KindProvider interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCQ) Kind() string {
+	return "PendingWorkloadsInClusterQueue"
+}
+
+// NewList implements rest.Lister interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCQ) NewList() runtime.Object {
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummaryList{}
+}
+
+// List implements rest.Lister interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCQ) List(ctx context.Context, options *metainternalversion.ListOptions) (runtime.Object, error) {
+	// TODO: consider returning error
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummaryList{}, nil
+}
+
+// Get implements rest.Getter interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCQ) Get(ctx context.Context, name string, opts *metav1.GetOptions) (runtime.Object, error) {
+	m.kueueMgr.UpdateSnapshot(name, WholeSnapshot)
```

  IIUC, updating the snapshot might be problematic, as this would cause the visibility in status to save this snapshot. 
  
  I think we could expose a new function by manager "ComputeHead(cqName, count) []*workload.Info". Then, call it from the new code. It means that the snapshot isn't updated, but I think this is ok. I think then the new function could also be reused by the existing code.

```diff
+		})
```

- **hack/update-helm.sh:103** by [@PBundyra](https://github.com/PBundyra) — 2023-10-30T09:23:45Z
```diff
@@ -92,3 +95,25 @@ for output_file in ${DEST_RBAC_DIR}/*.yaml; do
     $YQ -N -i '.subjects.[].namespace = "{{ .Release.Namespace }}"' $output_file
   fi
 done
+
+# Add visibility files, replace names, namespaces in helm format, remove document separators (---)
+for output_file in ${DEST_VISIBILITY_DIR}/*.yaml; do
+  if [ "$(cat $output_file | $YQ '.metadata | has("name")')" = "true" ] &&
+    [ "$(cat $output_file | $YQ '.metadata.name | (. == "v1alpha1*")')" = "false" ]; then
```

  It is, as the name of the APIService needs to remain unchanged.

### Review by [@PBundyra](https://github.com/PBundyra) (commented) — 2023-10-30T09:26:05Z

- **hack/update-helm.sh:108** by [@PBundyra](https://github.com/PBundyra) — 2023-10-30T09:26:05Z
```diff
@@ -92,3 +95,25 @@ for output_file in ${DEST_RBAC_DIR}/*.yaml; do
     $YQ -N -i '.subjects.[].namespace = "{{ .Release.Namespace }}"' $output_file
   fi
 done
+
+# Add visibility files, replace names, namespaces in helm format, remove document separators (---)
+for output_file in ${DEST_VISIBILITY_DIR}/*.yaml; do
+  if [ "$(cat $output_file | $YQ '.metadata | has("name")')" = "true" ] &&
+    [ "$(cat $output_file | $YQ '.metadata.name | (. == "v1alpha1*")')" = "false" ]; then
+    $YQ -N -i '.metadata.name |= "{{ include \"kueue.fullname\" . }}-" + .' $output_file
+  fi
+  if [ "$(cat $output_file | $YQ '.metadata | has("namespace")')" = "true" ] &&
+    [ "$(cat $output_file | $YQ '.metadata.namespace | (. == "kube-system")')" = "false" ]; then
```

  It is, as the namespace of the new RoleBinding needs to remain unchanged. I'll add a comment on that

```diff
+type pendingWorkloadsInCQ struct {
+	kueueMgr *queue.Manager
+	log      logr.Logger

+	WholeSnapshot = 100000

+var _ rest.KindProvider = &pendingWorkloadsInCQ{}
+var _ rest.Storage = &pendingWorkloadsInCQ{}
+var _ rest.Getter = &pendingWorkloadsInCQ{}

+// New implements rest.Storage interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCQ) New() runtime.Object {
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummary{}
+}
+
+// Destroy implements rest.Storage interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCQ) Destroy() {
+}
+
+// Kind implements rest.KindProvider interface

+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummaryList{}

+	// TODO: consider returning error
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummaryList{}, nil
+}
+
+// Get implements rest.Getter interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCQ) Get(ctx context.Context, name string, opts *metav1.GetOptions) (runtime.Object, error) {
+	m.kueueMgr.UpdateSnapshot(name, WholeSnapshot)
```
```diff
+	var wls []v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummary
+	for _, val := range m.kueueMgr.GetSnapshot(name) {
+		wls = append(wls, v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummary{
+			ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+				Name:      val.Name,
+				Namespace: val.Namespace,
+			},
+		})
+	}
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummaryList{Items: wls}, nil
+}
```

```diff
+// +genclient
+// +kubebuilder:object:root=true
+// +k8s:openapi-gen=true
+
+// User-facing representation of a pending workload that summarizes the relevant information for
+// position in the cluster queue.
+type PendingWorkloadSummary struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta   `json:",inline"`
+	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
+}
+
+// +kubebuilder:object:root=true
+// +k8s:openapi-gen=true
+
+// PendingWorkloadSummaryList contains a list of pending workloads in the context
+// of the query (within LocalQueue or ClusterQueue).
+type PendingWorkloadSummaryList struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta `json:",inline"`
+	metav1.ListMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
+
+	Items []PendingWorkloadSummary `json:"items"`
+}
+
+func init() {
+	SchemeBuilder.Register(&PendingWorkloadSummary{}, &PendingWorkloadSummaryList{})
```

  This looks odd compared to https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/blob/0adc8c45dabaf08eb72bc27877515841eaf0a1c4/apis/kueue/v1beta1/workload_types.go#L300
  
  In there, WorkloadList is used to list workloads, when the URL refers to workloads.
  
  In this case, the URL refers to clusterqueue, but the elements are workloads?

```diff
+	var wls []v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummary
+	for _, val := range m.kueueMgr.GetPendingWorkloadsInfo(name) {
+		wls = append(wls, v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummary{
+			ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+				Name:      val.Name,
+				Namespace: val.Namespace,
+			},
+		})
+	}
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummaryList{Items: wls}, nil
+}
+
+// ConvertToTable implements rest.TableConvertor interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCQ) ConvertToTable(ctx context.Context, object runtime.Object, tableOptions runtime.Object) (*metav1beta1.Table, error) {
```

  I think there are multiple interfaces that you don't need to implement if we don't support them.

### Review by [@PBundyra](https://github.com/PBundyra) (commented) — 2023-11-09T09:53:05Z

- **charts/kueue/templates/manager/manager.yaml:26** by [@PBundyra](https://github.com/PBundyra) — 2023-11-09T09:53:04Z
```diff
@@ -23,6 +23,7 @@ spec:
       - args:
         - --config=/controller_manager_config.yaml
         - --zap-log-level=2
+        - --cert-dir=/tmp
```

  This is the directory where the TLS certs are located. Without it, apiserver tries to create `apiserver.local.config/certificates` directory, but since it doesn't have sufficient permissions, it fails.

```diff
+// User-facing representation of a pending workload that summarizes the relevant information for
+// position in the cluster queue.
+type PendingWorkloadSummary struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta   `json:",inline"`
+	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
+}

+// +k8s:openapi-gen=true
+
+// PendingWorkloadSummaryList contains a list of pending workloads in the context
+// of the query (within LocalQueue or ClusterQueue).
+type PendingWorkloadSummaryList struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta `json:",inline"`
+	metav1.ListMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
+
+	Items []PendingWorkloadSummary `json:"items"`
+}
+
+func init() {
+	SchemeBuilder.Register(&PendingWorkloadSummary{}, &PendingWorkloadSummaryList{})
```

```diff
+package rest
+
+import (
+	"context"
+
+	"fmt"
+
+	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
+	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime"
+	"k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/rest"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+
+	v1alpha1 "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/api_extension/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/queue"
+
+	_ "k8s.io/metrics/pkg/apis/metrics/install"
+)
+
+type pendingWorkloadsInCqREST struct {
+	kueueMgr *queue.Manager
+	log      logr.Logger
+}
+
+// var _ rest.KindProvider = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+var _ rest.Storage = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+var _ rest.GetterWithOptions = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+var _ rest.Scoper = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+var _ rest.SingularNameProvider = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+
+func NewPendingWorkloadsInCqREST(kueueMgr *queue.Manager) *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST {
+	return &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{
+		kueueMgr: kueueMgr,
+		log:      ctrl.Log.WithName("pending-workload-in-cq"),
+	}
+}
+
+// New implements rest.Storage interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) New() runtime.Object {
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummary{}
+}
+
+// Destroy implements rest.Storage interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) Destroy() {
+}
+
+// Kind implements rest.KindProvider interface
+// func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) Kind() string {
+// return "PendingWorkloadsInClusterQueue"
+// }
+
+// Get implements rest.Getter interface
+// It fetches information about pending workloads and returns according to query params
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) Get(ctx context.Context, name string, opts runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error) {
+	pendingWorkloadOpts, ok := opts.(*v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadOptions)
+	if !ok {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("invalid options object: %#v", opts)
+	}
+	limit := pendingWorkloadOpts.Limit
+	offset := pendingWorkloadOpts.Offset
+
+	var wls []v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummary
+	for pos, val := range m.kueueMgr.GetPendingWorkloadsInfo(name) {
+		if pos > int(offset) && pos <= int(offset)+int(limit) {
```

  ```suggestion
  		if pos >= int(offset) && pos <= int(offset)+int(limit) {
  ```
  when offset=0, we don't want to skip any pending workloads, but return all.

```diff
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/queue"
+
+	_ "k8s.io/metrics/pkg/apis/metrics/install"
+)
+
+type pendingWorkloadsInCqREST struct {
+	kueueMgr *queue.Manager
+	log      logr.Logger
+}
+
+// var _ rest.KindProvider = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+var _ rest.Storage = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+var _ rest.GetterWithOptions = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+var _ rest.Scoper = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
```

```diff
+		log:      ctrl.Log.WithName("pending-workload-in-cq"),
+	}
+}
+
+// New implements rest.Storage interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) New() runtime.Object {
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummary{}
+}
+
+// Destroy implements rest.Storage interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) Destroy() {
+}
+
+// Kind implements rest.KindProvider interface
+// func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) Kind() string {
+// return "PendingWorkloadsInClusterQueue"
+// }
+
+// Get implements rest.Getter interface
+// It fetches information about pending workloads and returns according to query params
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) Get(ctx context.Context, name string, opts runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error) {
+	pendingWorkloadOpts, ok := opts.(*v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadOptions)
+	if !ok {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("invalid options object: %#v", opts)
+	}
+	limit := pendingWorkloadOpts.Limit
+	offset := pendingWorkloadOpts.Offset
+
+	var wls []v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummary
+	for pos, val := range m.kueueMgr.GetPendingWorkloadsInfo(name) {
+		if pos > int(offset) && pos <= int(offset)+int(limit) {
+			wls = append(wls, v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummary{
+				ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+					Name:      val.Name,
+					Namespace: val.Namespace,
+				},
+			})
+		}
+	}
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummaryList{Items: wls}, nil
+}
+
+// NewGetOptions creates a new options object
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) NewGetOptions() (runtime.Object, bool, string) {
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadOptions{
+		Limit:  1000,
```

  Do we need to specify the defaults here, even though we have `v1alpha1/defaults.go`?

```diff
+	}
+}
+
+// New implements rest.Storage interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) New() runtime.Object {
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummary{}

+// Destroy implements rest.Storage interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) Destroy() {
+}
+
+// Kind implements rest.KindProvider interface
+// func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) Kind() string {
+// return "PendingWorkloadsInClusterQueue"

+// Get implements rest.Getter interface
+// It fetches information about pending workloads and returns according to query params
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) Get(ctx context.Context, name string, opts runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error) {
+	pendingWorkloadOpts, ok := opts.(*v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadOptions)
+	if !ok {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("invalid options object: %#v", opts)
+	}
+	limit := pendingWorkloadOpts.Limit
+	offset := pendingWorkloadOpts.Offset
+
+	var wls []v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummary
+	for pos, val := range m.kueueMgr.GetPendingWorkloadsInfo(name) {
+		if pos > int(offset) && pos <= int(offset)+int(limit) {
+			wls = append(wls, v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummary{
+				ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+					Name:      val.Name,
+					Namespace: val.Namespace,
+				},
+			})
+		}
+	}
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummaryList{Items: wls}, nil
+}
```

```diff
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadOptions{
+		Limit:  1000,
```

  I see, so if you just returned `v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadOptions{}` it would not be defaulted? In that case, I would suggest we expose `DefaultPendingWorkloadsLimit = 1000` in `pkg/constants/constants.go``?

```diff
+	setupLog = ctrl.Log.WithName("Visibility-server")
+)
+
+type server struct {
+	*genericapiserver.GenericAPIServer
+}
+
+// CreateAndStartVisibilityServer creates visibility server injecting KueueManager and starts it
+func CreateAndStartVisibilityServer(kueueMgr *queue.Manager) {
+	config := newVisibilityServerConfig()
+	if err := applyVisibilityServerOptions(config); err != nil {
+		setupLog.Error(err, "Unable to apply VisibilityServerOptions")
+	}
+
+	visibilityServer, err := config.Complete().New("visibility-server", genericapiserver.NewEmptyDelegate())
+	if err != nil {
+		setupLog.Error(err, "Unable to create visibility server")
+	}
+
+	if err := api.Install(visibilityServer, kueueMgr); err != nil {
+		setupLog.Error(err, "Unable to install visibility.kueue.x-k8s.io/v1alpha1 API")
+
```

```diff
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+/*
+This file is needed for kubernetes/code-generator/kube_codegen.sh script used in hack/update-codegen.sh.
+*/
+
+package v1alpha1
+
+import (
+	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
+)
+
+// +genclient
+// +kubebuilder:object:root=true
+// +k8s:openapi-gen=true
+
+// PendingWorkload is a user-facing representation of a pending workload that summarizes the relevant information for
+// position in the cluster queue.
+type PendingWorkload struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta   `json:",inline"`
+	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
+}
+
+// +kubebuilder:object:root=true
+// +k8s:openapi-gen=true
+
+// PendingWorkloadList contains a list of pending workloads in the context
+// of the query (within LocalQueue or ClusterQueue).
+type PendingWorkloadList struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta `json:",inline"`
+	metav1.ListMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
+
+	Items []PendingWorkload `json:"items"`
+}
+
+// +kubebuilder:object:root=true
+// +k8s:openapi-gen=true
+// +k8s:conversion-gen:explicit-from=net/url.Values
+// +k8s:defaulter-gen=true
+
+// PendingWorkloadOptions are query params used in the visibility queries
+type PendingWorkloadOptions struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta `json:",inline"`
+
+	// Offset indicates position of the first pending workload that should be fetched starting from 0
+	Offset int64 `json:"offset"`
+
+	// Limit indicates max number of pending workloads that should be fetched
+	Limit int64 `json:"limit"`
```

  ```suggestion
  	Limit int64 `json:"limit, omitempty"`
  ```

  Good point, I'm not aware of such rules. Here is a couple of sub-resources registered by the core k8s:
  https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/blob/a00ea0df3599e989bf95692c4d425605a998ac84/pkg/registry/core/rest/storage_core.go#L231-L244. Looking at the `ephemeralcontainers` plural is ok, but we probably should make it just `pendingworkloads` (without _). 
  
  Similarly, in the endpoint names we have "localqueues" (without _, nor -).

```diff
+	"context"
+
+	"fmt"
+
+	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
+	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime"
+	"k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/rest"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+
+	v1alpha1 "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/api_extension/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/queue"
+
+	_ "k8s.io/metrics/pkg/apis/metrics/install"
+)
+
+type pendingWorkloadsInCqREST struct {
+	kueueMgr *queue.Manager
+	log      logr.Logger
+}
+
+// var _ rest.KindProvider = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+var _ rest.Storage = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+var _ rest.GetterWithOptions = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+var _ rest.Scoper = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+var _ rest.SingularNameProvider = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+
+func NewPendingWorkloadsInCqREST(kueueMgr *queue.Manager) *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST {
+	return &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{
+		kueueMgr: kueueMgr,
+		log:      ctrl.Log.WithName("pending-workload-in-cq"),
+	}
+}
+
+// New implements rest.Storage interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) New() runtime.Object {
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummary{}
+}
+
+// Destroy implements rest.Storage interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) Destroy() {
+}
+
+// Kind implements rest.KindProvider interface
+// func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) Kind() string {
+// return "PendingWorkloadsInClusterQueue"
+// }
+
+// Get implements rest.Getter interface
+// It fetches information about pending workloads and returns according to query params
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) Get(ctx context.Context, name string, opts runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error) {
+	pendingWorkloadOpts, ok := opts.(*v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadOptions)
+	if !ok {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("invalid options object: %#v", opts)
+	}
+	limit := pendingWorkloadOpts.Limit
+	offset := pendingWorkloadOpts.Offset
+
+	var wls []v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummary
+	for pos, val := range m.kueueMgr.GetPendingWorkloadsInfo(name) {
+		if pos > int(offset) && pos <= int(offset)+int(limit) {
+			wls = append(wls, v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummary{
+				ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+					Name:      val.Name,
+					Namespace: val.Namespace,
+				},
+			})
+		}
+	}
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadSummaryList{Items: wls}, nil
+}
+
+// NewGetOptions creates a new options object
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) NewGetOptions() (runtime.Object, bool, string) {
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadOptions{
+		Limit:  1000,
```

  > so if you just returned `v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadOptions{}` it would not be defaulted?
  
  Exactly
  > we expose DefaultPendingWorkloadsLimit = 1000 in `pkg/constants/constants.go`
  
  Thanks, I'll add that

- **pkg/visibility/server.go:71** by [@PBundyra](https://github.com/PBundyra) — 2023-11-14T13:25:36Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,105 @@
+// Copyright 2023 The Kubernetes Authors.
+//
+// Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+// you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+// You may obtain a copy of the License at
+//
+//     http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
+//
+// Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+// distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+// WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+// See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+// limitations under the License.
+
+package visibility
+
+import (
+	"context"
+	"fmt"
+	"net"
+	"strings"
+
+	genericapiserver "k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server"
+	genericoptions "k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options"
+
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/visibility/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/queue"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/visibility/api"
+
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+
+	openapinamer "k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/openapi"
+	"k8s.io/client-go/pkg/version"
+	_ "k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/restclient" // for client-go metrics registration
+
+	generatedopenapi "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/visibility/v1alpha1/openapi"
+)
+
+var (
+	setupLog = ctrl.Log.WithName("Visibility-server")
+)
+
+type server struct {
+	*genericapiserver.GenericAPIServer
+}
+
+// CreateAndStartVisibilityServer creates visibility server injecting KueueManager and starts it
+func CreateAndStartVisibilityServer(kueueMgr *queue.Manager) {
+	config := newVisibilityServerConfig()
+	if err := applyVisibilityServerOptions(config); err != nil {
+		setupLog.Error(err, "Unable to apply VisibilityServerOptions")
+	}
+
+	visibilityServer, err := config.Complete().New("visibility-server", genericapiserver.NewEmptyDelegate())
+	if err != nil {
+		setupLog.Error(err, "Unable to create visibility server")
+	}
+
+	if err := api.Install(visibilityServer, kueueMgr); err != nil {
+		setupLog.Error(err, "Unable to install visibility.kueue.x-k8s.io/v1alpha1 API")
+
+	}
+
+	s := &server{visibilityServer}
+	if err := s.runUntil(genericapiserver.SetupSignalHandler()); err != nil {
+		setupLog.Error(err, "Error running visibility server")
+	}
+}
+
+// runUntil runs underlying genericapiserver until stopCh is closed
+func (s *server) runUntil(stopCh <-chan struct{}) error {
+	_, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())
+	defer cancel()
+	return s.GenericAPIServer.PrepareRun().Run(stopCh)
+}
+
+func applyVisibilityServerOptions(config *genericapiserver.RecommendedConfig) error {
+	o := genericoptions.NewRecommendedOptions("", api.Codecs.LegacyCodec(v1alpha1.SchemeGroupVersion))
+	o.Etcd = nil
+	o.SecureServing.BindPort = 8082
+	// The directory where TLS certs will be created
+	o.SecureServing.ServerCert.CertDirectory = "/tmp"
```

  Please let me know what you think about this solution @alculquicondor. It is an alternative to passing this variable as a flag

- **apis/visibility/v1alpha1/openapi/zz_generated.openapi.go:1** by [@PBundyra](https://github.com/PBundyra) — 2023-11-15T09:13:14Z
  I am afraid we need it as it is necessary to use the `apiserver` framework. `openapi` package is generated by `kube::codegen`  so unless we manually move the `zz_generated.openapi.go` file there is not much we can do. `metrics-server` does the same:
  https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/metrics-server/tree/master/pkg/api/generated/openapi

- **apis/visibility/v1alpha1/conversion/conversion_test.go:1** by [@PBundyra](https://github.com/PBundyra) — 2023-11-15T09:19:17Z
  The reasoning behind creating this new package was to avoid a dependency cycle. The test uses `pkg/visibility/api` that uses `apis/visibility/v1alpha1` so it's not possible for the test file to `apis/visibility/v1alpha1`. I can move it to `pkg/visibility/api` if you think it's a better idea

```diff
+	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`

+// +k8s:openapi-gen=true
+// +k8s:conversion-gen:explicit-from=net/url.Values
+// +k8s:defaulter-gen=true
+
+// PendingWorkloadOptions are query params used in the visibility queries
+type PendingWorkloadOptions struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta `json:",inline"`
+
+	// Offset indicates position of the first pending workload that should be fetched starting from 0. 0 by default
+	Offset int64 `json:"offset"`
+
+	// Limit indicates max number of pending workloads that should be fetched. 1000 by default
+	Limit int64 `json:"limit,omitempty"`
+}

+		&PendingWorkload{},
```

```diff
+package rest
+
+import (
+	"context"
+	"fmt"
+
+	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
+	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"

+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/queue"
+
+	_ "k8s.io/metrics/pkg/apis/metrics/install"
+)
+
+type pendingWorkloadsInCqREST struct {
+	kueueMgr *queue.Manager
+	log      logr.Logger
+}
+
+var _ rest.Storage = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+var _ rest.GetterWithOptions = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+var _ rest.Scoper = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+var _ rest.SingularNameProvider = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+
+func NewPendingWorkloadsInCqREST(kueueMgr *queue.Manager) *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST {
+	return &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{
+		kueueMgr: kueueMgr,
+		log:      ctrl.Log.WithName("pending-workload-in-cq"),
+	}
+}
+
+// New implements rest.Storage interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) New() runtime.Object {
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadList{}
+}
+
+// Destroy implements rest.Storage interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) Destroy() {}
+
+// Get implements rest.Getter interface
+// It fetches information about pending workloads and returns according to query params
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) Get(ctx context.Context, name string, opts runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error) {
+	pendingWorkloadOpts, ok := opts.(*v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadOptions)
+	if !ok {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("invalid options object: %#v", opts)
+	}
+	limit := pendingWorkloadOpts.Limit
+	offset := pendingWorkloadOpts.Offset
+
+	var wls []v1alpha1.PendingWorkload
+	for index, val := range m.kueueMgr.GetPendingWorkloadsInfo(name) {
```

  For readability, and to avoid unnecessary iterations:
  ```golang
  for index := offset; index < offset+limit; index++
  ```

```diff
+
+	"github.com/go-logr/logr"
+	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime"
+	"k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/rest"
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+
+	v1alpha1 "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/visibility/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/constants"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/queue"
+
+	_ "k8s.io/metrics/pkg/apis/metrics/install"
+)
+
+type pendingWorkloadsInCqREST struct {
+	kueueMgr *queue.Manager
+	log      logr.Logger
+}
+
+var _ rest.Storage = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+var _ rest.GetterWithOptions = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+var _ rest.Scoper = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+var _ rest.SingularNameProvider = &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{}
+
+func NewPendingWorkloadsInCqREST(kueueMgr *queue.Manager) *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST {
+	return &pendingWorkloadsInCqREST{
+		kueueMgr: kueueMgr,
+		log:      ctrl.Log.WithName("pending-workload-in-cq"),
+	}
+}
+
+// New implements rest.Storage interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) New() runtime.Object {
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadList{}
+}
+
+// Destroy implements rest.Storage interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) Destroy() {}
+
+// Get implements rest.Getter interface
+// It fetches information about pending workloads and returns according to query params
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) Get(ctx context.Context, name string, opts runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error) {
+	pendingWorkloadOpts, ok := opts.(*v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadOptions)
+	if !ok {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("invalid options object: %#v", opts)
+	}
+	limit := pendingWorkloadOpts.Limit
+	offset := pendingWorkloadOpts.Offset
+
+	var wls []v1alpha1.PendingWorkload
+	for index, val := range m.kueueMgr.GetPendingWorkloadsInfo(name) {
+		if index >= int(offset) && index < int(offset)+int(limit) {
+			wls = append(wls, v1alpha1.PendingWorkload{
+				ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+					Name:      val.Name,
+					Namespace: val.Namespace,
+				},
+			})
+		}
+	}
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadList{Items: wls}, nil
+}
+
+// NewGetOptions creates a new options object
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) NewGetOptions() (runtime.Object, bool, string) {
+	// If no query parameters were passed the generated defaults function are not executed so it's necessary to set default values here as well
+	return &v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadOptions{
+		Limit: constants.DefaultPendingWorkloadsLimit,
+	}, false, ""
+}
+
+// NamespaceScoped implements rest.Scoper interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) NamespaceScoped() bool {
+	return false
+}
+
+// GetSingularName implements rest.SingularNameProvider interface
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) GetSingularName() string {
+	return "pendingWorkloadsInCQ"
```

  just to make sure we are being consistent... which name does the pods/log subresource use?

- **pkg/visibility/server.go:71** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-11-15T18:53:47Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,105 @@
+// Copyright 2023 The Kubernetes Authors.
+//
+// Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+// you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+// You may obtain a copy of the License at
+//

+// WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+// See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+// limitations under the License.
+
+package visibility
+
+import (
+	"context"
+	"fmt"
+	"net"
+	"strings"
+
+	genericapiserver "k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server"
+	genericoptions "k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options"
+
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/visibility/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/queue"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/visibility/api"
+
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+
+	openapinamer "k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/openapi"
+	"k8s.io/client-go/pkg/version"
+	_ "k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/restclient" // for client-go metrics registration
+
+	generatedopenapi "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/visibility/v1alpha1/openapi"
+)
+
+var (
+	setupLog = ctrl.Log.WithName("Visibility-server")
+)
+
+type server struct {
+	*genericapiserver.GenericAPIServer
+}
+
+// CreateAndStartVisibilityServer creates visibility server injecting KueueManager and starts it
+func CreateAndStartVisibilityServer(kueueMgr *queue.Manager) {
+	config := newVisibilityServerConfig()
+	if err := applyVisibilityServerOptions(config); err != nil {
+		setupLog.Error(err, "Unable to apply VisibilityServerOptions")
+	}
+
+	visibilityServer, err := config.Complete().New("visibility-server", genericapiserver.NewEmptyDelegate())
+	if err != nil {
+		setupLog.Error(err, "Unable to create visibility server")
+	}
+
+	if err := api.Install(visibilityServer, kueueMgr); err != nil {
+		setupLog.Error(err, "Unable to install visibility.kueue.x-k8s.io/v1alpha1 API")
+
+	}
+
+	s := &server{visibilityServer}
+	if err := s.runUntil(genericapiserver.SetupSignalHandler()); err != nil {
+		setupLog.Error(err, "Error running visibility server")
+	}
+}
+
+// runUntil runs underlying genericapiserver until stopCh is closed
+func (s *server) runUntil(stopCh <-chan struct{}) error {
+	_, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())
+	defer cancel()
+	return s.GenericAPIServer.PrepareRun().Run(stopCh)
+}
+
+func applyVisibilityServerOptions(config *genericapiserver.RecommendedConfig) error {
+	o := genericoptions.NewRecommendedOptions("", api.Codecs.LegacyCodec(v1alpha1.SchemeGroupVersion))
+	o.Etcd = nil
+	o.SecureServing.BindPort = 8082
+	// The directory where TLS certs will be created
+	o.SecureServing.ServerCert.CertDirectory = "/tmp"
```

  and this is the same that metrics-server does, right?


  All subresources use a name inherited from the parent resource. This name is used to create correct reports and to access resources from kubectl. Hence, I'll move it to the `CqREST` implementation. Even if it may not be directly used there, it will span across all its subresources which may be useful.


  Setting `/tmp` as CertDirectory is the default configuration for metrics-server. However, they allow the user to change it with a flag: 
  https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/metrics-server/blob/6242212f633d50d6066d2fe95f221b052ef4e1ae/manifests/base/deployment.yaml#L24
  
  This is only used when the user doesn't provide certificates and doesn't prevent the user from doing so

```diff
+
+// Get implements rest.Getter interface
+// It fetches information about pending workloads and returns according to query params
+func (m *pendingWorkloadsInCqREST) Get(ctx context.Context, name string, opts runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error) {
+	pendingWorkloadOpts, ok := opts.(*v1alpha1.PendingWorkloadOptions)
+	if !ok {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("invalid options object: %#v", opts)
+	}
+	limit := pendingWorkloadOpts.Limit
+	offset := pendingWorkloadOpts.Offset
+
+	var wls []v1alpha1.PendingWorkload
```

  ```suggestion
  	wls := make([]v1alpha1.PendingWorkload, 0, offset)
  ```

```diff
+// Copyright 2023 The Kubernetes Authors.
```

```diff
+// WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+// See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+// limitations under the License.
+
+package visibility
+
+import (
+	"context"
+	"fmt"
+	"net"
+	"strings"
+
+	genericapiserver "k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server"
+	genericoptions "k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options"
+
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/visibility/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/queue"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/visibility/api"
+
+	ctrl "sigs.k8s.io/controller-runtime"
+
+	openapinamer "k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/openapi"
+	"k8s.io/client-go/pkg/version"
+	_ "k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/restclient" // for client-go metrics registration
+
+	generatedopenapi "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/apis/visibility/v1alpha1/openapi"
+)
+
+var (
+	setupLog = ctrl.Log.WithName("visibility-server")
+)
+
+type server struct {
+	*genericapiserver.GenericAPIServer
+}
+
+// CreateAndStartVisibilityServer creates visibility server injecting KueueManager and starts it
+func CreateAndStartVisibilityServer(kueueMgr *queue.Manager) {
+	config := newVisibilityServerConfig()
+	if err := applyVisibilityServerOptions(config); err != nil {
+		setupLog.Error(err, "Unable to apply VisibilityServerOptions")
+	}
+
+	visibilityServer, err := config.Complete().New("visibility-server", genericapiserver.NewEmptyDelegate())
+	if err != nil {
+		setupLog.Error(err, "Unable to create visibility server")
+	}
+
+	if err := api.Install(visibilityServer, kueueMgr); err != nil {
+		setupLog.Error(err, "Unable to install visibility.kueue.x-k8s.io/v1alpha1 API")
+	}
+
+	s := &server{visibilityServer}
+	if err := s.runUntil(genericapiserver.SetupSignalHandler()); err != nil {
+		setupLog.Error(err, "Error running visibility server")
+	}
+}
+
+// runUntil runs underlying genericapiserver until stopCh is closed
+func (s *server) runUntil(stopCh <-chan struct{}) error {
+	_, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())
```

  use the main kueue context, instead of `context.Background()`

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2023-11-21T18:13:18Z

- **test/e2e/e2e_test.go:94** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-11-21T18:10:43Z

```diff
+var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Kueue visibility server", func() {
+	const defaultFlavor = "default-flavor"
+	var (
+		defaultRF    *kueue.ResourceFlavor
+		localQueue   *kueue.LocalQueue
+		clusterQueue *kueue.ClusterQueue
+		ns           *corev1.Namespace
+		sampleJob1   *batchv1.Job
+		sampleJob2   *batchv1.Job
+	)
+
+	ginkgo.BeforeEach(func() {
+		ns = &corev1.Namespace{
+			ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+				GenerateName: "e2e-",
+			},
+		}
+		gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, ns)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+
+		defaultRF = testing.MakeResourceFlavor(defaultFlavor).Obj()
+		gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, defaultRF)).Should(gomega.Succeed())

+				*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas(defaultFlavor).

+					Obj(),
+			).Obj()
+		gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, clusterQueue)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+

+		gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, localQueue)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+	})
+	ginkgo.AfterEach(func() {
+		gomega.Expect(util.DeleteNamespace(ctx, k8sClient, ns)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+		gomega.Expect(util.DeleteLocalQueue(ctx, k8sClient, localQueue)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+		util.ExpectClusterQueueToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, clusterQueue, true)
+		util.ExpectResourceFlavorToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, defaultRF, true)
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.When("Creating two Jobs with max capacity", func() {
+		ginkgo.BeforeEach(func() {
+			sampleJob1 = testingjob.MakeJob("test-job-1", ns.Name).
+				Queue(localQueue.Name).
+				Image("gcr.io/k8s-staging-perf-tests/sleep:v0.0.3", []string{"3s"}).
+				Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "1").
+				Obj()
+			sampleJob2 = testingjob.MakeJob("test-job-2", ns.Name).
+				Queue(localQueue.Name).
+				Image("gcr.io/k8s-staging-perf-tests/sleep:v0.0.3", []string{"100ms"}).
+				Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "1").
+				Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, sampleJob1)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, sampleJob2)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+		})
+		ginkgo.AfterEach(func() {
+			gomega.Expect(util.DeleteAllJobsInNamespace(ctx, k8sClient, ns)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+		})
+
+		ginkgo.It("Should fetch information about pending workloads", func() {
```

  I'm a little bit worried about the 3s runtime of a job, if the test could flake on some heavily loaded environments. 
  
  Maybe we could have a little more confidence in stability with the following scenario:
  - verify the pending workloads are empty
  - schedule `sampleJob1` which runs forever, it gets admitted and blocks quota
  - schedule `sampleJob2` which is queued as pending
  - verify we have a single job pending
  - delete `sampleJob1` by delete request, so that if frees the resources, allowing for `sampleJob2` to get admitted
  - verify the list of pending workloads is empty once `sampleJob2` is admitted

```diff
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "1").
+					PriorityClass(highPriorityClass.Name).
+					Obj()

+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "1").
+					PriorityClass(lowPriorityClass.Name).
```

```diff
+			util.ExpectClusterQueueToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, clusterQueue, true)
+			util.ExpectResourceFlavorToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, defaultRF, true)
+		})
+

+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(sampleJob1), createdJob)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					return int(*createdJob.Status.Ready)
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Equal(1))
+				// Make sure that pod can receive SIGTERM
+				time.Sleep(time.Second * 1)
+			})
```

```diff
+				lowPriorityClass := testing.MakePriorityClass("low").PriorityValue(50).Obj()
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, lowPriorityClass))
+				ginkgo.DeferCleanup(func() {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Delete(ctx, lowPriorityClass)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				sampleJob1 = testingjob.MakeJob("test-job-1", ns.Name).
+					Queue(localQueue.Name).
+					Image("gcr.io/k8s-staging-perf-tests/sleep:v0.0.3", []string{"60s", "-termination-grace-period", "0s"}).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "1").
+					PriorityClass(highPriorityClass.Name).
+					Obj()
+				sampleJob2 = testingjob.MakeJob("test-job-2", ns.Name).
+					Queue(localQueue.Name).
+					Image("gcr.io/k8s-staging-perf-tests/sleep:v0.0.3", []string{"1ms"}).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "1").
+					PriorityClass(lowPriorityClass.Name).
+					Obj()
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, sampleJob1)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, sampleJob2)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("Have one pending workload", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func() int {
+					info, err := visibilityClient.ClusterQueues().GetPendingWorkloadsSummary(ctx, clusterQueue.Name, metav1.GetOptions{})
+					gomega.Expect(err).NotTo(gomega.HaveOccurred())
+					return len(info.Items)
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Equal(1))
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("Await for pods to be running", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func() int {
+					createdJob := &batchv1.Job{}
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(sampleJob1), createdJob)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					return int(*createdJob.Status.Ready)
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Equal(1))
+				// Make sure that pod can receive SIGTERM
+				time.Sleep(time.Second * 1)
```

  why is the sleep necessary? Is it because the Pod might not have registered for the SIGTERM yet?

```diff
+

+				ResourceGroup(
+					*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas(defaultFlavor).
+						Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "1").
+						Obj(),
+				).
+				Preemption(kueue.ClusterQueuePreemption{
+					WithinClusterQueue: kueue.PreemptionPolicyLowerPriority,
+				}).
+				Obj()

+		ginkgo.AfterEach(func() {
+			gomega.Expect(util.DeleteLocalQueue(ctx, k8sClient, localQueue)).Should(gomega.Succeed())

+			util.ExpectClusterQueueToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, clusterQueue, true)
+			util.ExpectResourceFlavorToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, defaultRF, true)
+		})

+			})

+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Delete(ctx, highPriorityClass)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+				})

+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Delete(ctx, lowPriorityClass)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+				})

+					Image("gcr.io/k8s-staging-perf-tests/sleep:v0.0.3", []string{"60s", "-termination-grace-period", "0s"}).

+					PriorityClass(highPriorityClass.Name).
+					Obj()
+				sampleJob2 = testingjob.MakeJob("test-job-2", ns.Name).
+					Queue(localQueue.Name).
+					Image("gcr.io/k8s-staging-perf-tests/sleep:v0.0.3", []string{"1ms"}).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "1").
+					PriorityClass(lowPriorityClass.Name).
+					Obj()

```

  We tried to fix it without sleep, and send Delete (SIGTERM) to the running pod, but it some case the pod terminated only after 20-30s (probably due to SIGKILL).
  
  We think so, when repeated 50times, we got error rate about 10%, but haven't pinned down the root cause exactly.

```diff
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "1").
+					PriorityClass(highPriorityClass.Name).
+					Obj()
+				sampleJob2 = testingjob.MakeJob("test-job-2", ns.Name).
+					Queue(localQueue.Name).
+					Image("gcr.io/k8s-staging-perf-tests/sleep:v0.0.3", []string{"1ms"}).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "1").
+					PriorityClass(lowPriorityClass.Name).
+					Obj()
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, sampleJob1)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, sampleJob2)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("Have one pending workload", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func() int {
+					info, err := visibilityClient.ClusterQueues().GetPendingWorkloadsSummary(ctx, clusterQueue.Name, metav1.GetOptions{})
+					gomega.Expect(err).NotTo(gomega.HaveOccurred())
+					return len(info.Items)
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Equal(1))
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("Await for pods to be running", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func() int {
+					createdJob := &batchv1.Job{}
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(sampleJob1), createdJob)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					return int(*createdJob.Status.Ready)
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Equal(1))
+				// Make sure that pod can receive SIGTERM
+				time.Sleep(time.Second * 1)
```

  I'm fine with the 5s delay for now, as long as we create a issue to follow up.

```diff
+var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Kueue visibility server", func() {
+	const defaultFlavor = "default-flavor"
+	var (
+		defaultRF    *kueue.ResourceFlavor
+		localQueue   *kueue.LocalQueue
+		clusterQueue *kueue.ClusterQueue
+		ns           *corev1.Namespace
+		sampleJob1   *batchv1.Job
+		sampleJob2   *batchv1.Job
+	)
+
+	ginkgo.BeforeEach(func() {
+		ns = &corev1.Namespace{
+			ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+				GenerateName: "e2e-",
+			},
+		}
+		gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, ns)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+	})
+	ginkgo.AfterEach(func() {
+		gomega.Expect(util.DeleteNamespace(ctx, k8sClient, ns)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.When("Creating two Jobs with max capacity", func() {
+		ginkgo.BeforeEach(func() {
+			defaultRF = testing.MakeResourceFlavor(defaultFlavor).Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, defaultRF)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+
+			clusterQueue = testing.MakeClusterQueue("cluster-queue").
+				ResourceGroup(
+					*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas(defaultFlavor).
+						Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "1").
+						Obj(),
+				).
+				Preemption(kueue.ClusterQueuePreemption{
+					WithinClusterQueue: kueue.PreemptionPolicyLowerPriority,
+				}).
+				Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, clusterQueue)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+
+			localQueue = testing.MakeLocalQueue("main", ns.Name).ClusterQueue(clusterQueue.Name).Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, localQueue)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+
+		})
+		ginkgo.AfterEach(func() {
+			gomega.Expect(util.DeleteLocalQueue(ctx, k8sClient, localQueue)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			gomega.Expect(util.DeleteAllJobsInNamespace(ctx, k8sClient, ns)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			util.ExpectClusterQueueToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, clusterQueue, true)
+			util.ExpectResourceFlavorToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, defaultRF, true)
+		})
+
+		ginkgo.It("Should fetch information about pending workloads", func() {
+			ginkgo.By("Have zero pending workloads", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func() int {
+					info, err := visibilityClient.ClusterQueues().GetPendingWorkloadsSummary(ctx, clusterQueue.Name, metav1.GetOptions{})
+					gomega.Expect(err).NotTo(gomega.HaveOccurred())
+					return len(info.Items)
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Equal(0))
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("Schedule two max capacity jobs", func() {
+				highPriorityClass := testing.MakePriorityClass("high").PriorityValue(100).Obj()
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, highPriorityClass))
+				ginkgo.DeferCleanup(func() {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Delete(ctx, highPriorityClass)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				lowPriorityClass := testing.MakePriorityClass("low").PriorityValue(50).Obj()
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, lowPriorityClass))
+				ginkgo.DeferCleanup(func() {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Delete(ctx, lowPriorityClass)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				sampleJob1 = testingjob.MakeJob("test-job-1", ns.Name).
+					Queue(localQueue.Name).
+					Image("gcr.io/k8s-staging-perf-tests/sleep:v0.0.3", []string{"60s", "-termination-grace-period", "0s"}).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "1").
+					PriorityClass(highPriorityClass.Name).
+					Obj()
+				sampleJob2 = testingjob.MakeJob("test-job-2", ns.Name).
+					Queue(localQueue.Name).
+					Image("gcr.io/k8s-staging-perf-tests/sleep:v0.0.3", []string{"1ms"}).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "1").
+					PriorityClass(lowPriorityClass.Name).
+					Obj()
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, sampleJob1)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, sampleJob2)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("Have one pending workload", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func() int {
+					info, err := visibilityClient.ClusterQueues().GetPendingWorkloadsSummary(ctx, clusterQueue.Name, metav1.GetOptions{})
+					gomega.Expect(err).NotTo(gomega.HaveOccurred())
+					return len(info.Items)
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Equal(1))
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("Await for pods to be running", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func() int {
+					createdJob := &batchv1.Job{}
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(sampleJob1), createdJob)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					return int(*createdJob.Status.Ready)
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Equal(1))
+				// Make sure that pod can receive SIGTERM
+				time.Sleep(time.Second * 1)
```

  I think 1s delay should be enough. We are only calling Delete once the Job reports `status.ready=1`. This would only happen if the Pod is already running, as observed by kubelet.

```diff
+					info, err := visibilityClient.ClusterQueues().GetPendingWorkloadsSummary(ctx, clusterQueue.Name, metav1.GetOptions{})
+					gomega.Expect(err).NotTo(gomega.HaveOccurred())
+					return len(info.Items)
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Equal(1))
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("Await for pods to be running", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func() int {
+					createdJob := &batchv1.Job{}
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, client.ObjectKeyFromObject(sampleJob1), createdJob)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					return int(*createdJob.Status.Ready)
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Equal(1))
+				// Make sure that pod can receive SIGTERM
+				time.Sleep(time.Second * 1)
```

  @alculquicondor WDYT?

```diff
+			util.ExpectClusterQueueToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, clusterQueue, true)

+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Delete(ctx, highPriorityClass)).To(gomega.Succeed())

+					Queue(localQueue.Name).
+					Image("gcr.io/k8s-staging-perf-tests/sleep:v0.0.3", []string{"60s", "-termination-grace-period", "0s"}).

+					PriorityClass(highPriorityClass.Name).
+					Obj()

+					Queue(localQueue.Name).
+					Image("gcr.io/k8s-staging-perf-tests/sleep:v0.0.3", []string{"1ms"}).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "1").
+					PriorityClass(lowPriorityClass.Name).
```

  Still worth waiting for status.ready==1, and maybe a 3s sleep?
  
  I'm fine with 3s, but suggest to go with 5s as a temporary solution, because 5s is already used in other tests, so for consistency. Then, I think we should open an issue to review the tests and shorten the execution times. We confirmed with @PBundyra that some other tests are sensitive to the 5s delay.
  
  I'm not sure there is point waiting for `status.ready=1` if we are not going to delete the pod (in the proposed solution), we just wait for the pod to complete.

- **test/e2e/e2e_test.go:128** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-11-23T07:41:41Z
```diff
@@ -38,6 +38,131 @@ import (
 
 // +kubebuilder:docs-gen:collapse=Imports
 
+var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Kueue visibility server", func() {
+	const defaultFlavor = "default-flavor"
+	var (
+		defaultRF    *kueue.ResourceFlavor
+		localQueue   *kueue.LocalQueue
+		clusterQueue *kueue.ClusterQueue
+		ns           *corev1.Namespace
+		sampleJob1   *batchv1.Job
+		sampleJob2   *batchv1.Job
+	)
+
+	ginkgo.BeforeEach(func() {
+		ns = &corev1.Namespace{
+			ObjectMeta: metav1.ObjectMeta{
+				GenerateName: "e2e-",
+			},
+		}
+		gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, ns)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+	})
+	ginkgo.AfterEach(func() {
+		gomega.Expect(util.DeleteNamespace(ctx, k8sClient, ns)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.When("There are pending workloads due to max capacity by the admitted job", func() {
+		ginkgo.BeforeEach(func() {
+			defaultRF = testing.MakeResourceFlavor(defaultFlavor).Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, defaultRF)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+
+			clusterQueue = testing.MakeClusterQueue("cluster-queue").
+				ResourceGroup(
+					*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas(defaultFlavor).
+						Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "1").
+						Obj(),
+				).
+				Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, clusterQueue)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+
+			localQueue = testing.MakeLocalQueue("main", ns.Name).ClusterQueue(clusterQueue.Name).Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, localQueue)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+
+		})
+		ginkgo.AfterEach(func() {
+			gomega.Expect(util.DeleteLocalQueue(ctx, k8sClient, localQueue)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			gomega.Expect(util.DeleteAllJobsInNamespace(ctx, k8sClient, ns)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			util.ExpectClusterQueueToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, clusterQueue, true)
+			util.ExpectResourceFlavorToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, defaultRF, true)
+		})
+
+		ginkgo.It("Should allow fetching information about pending workloads", func() {
+			ginkgo.By("Verify there are zero pending workloads", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func() int {
+					info, err := visibilityClient.ClusterQueues().GetPendingWorkloadsSummary(ctx, clusterQueue.Name, metav1.GetOptions{})
+					gomega.Expect(err).NotTo(gomega.HaveOccurred())
+					return len(info.Items)
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Equal(0))
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("Schedule a job that when admitted blocks the queue", func() {
+				highPriorityClass := testing.MakePriorityClass("high").PriorityValue(100).Obj()
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, highPriorityClass))
+				ginkgo.DeferCleanup(func() {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Delete(ctx, highPriorityClass)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				sampleJob1 = testingjob.MakeJob("test-job-1", ns.Name).
+					Queue(localQueue.Name).
+					Image("gcr.io/k8s-staging-perf-tests/sleep:v0.0.3", []string{"60s", "-termination-grace-period", "0s"}).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "1").
+					TerimnationGracePeriod(1).
+					BackoffLimit(0).
+					PriorityClass(highPriorityClass.Name).
+					Obj()
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, sampleJob1)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("Schedule a job which is pending due to lower priority", func() {
+				lowPriorityClass := testing.MakePriorityClass("low").PriorityValue(50).Obj()
+				gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, lowPriorityClass))
+				ginkgo.DeferCleanup(func() {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Delete(ctx, lowPriorityClass)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+				})
+
+				sampleJob2 = testingjob.MakeJob("test-job-2", ns.Name).
+					Queue(localQueue.Name).
+					Image("gcr.io/k8s-staging-perf-tests/sleep:v0.0.3", []string{"1ms"}).

+					TerimnationGracePeriod(1).
```

  `terminationGracePedriod` and `backoffLimit` should not be needed for this job.

- **test/e2e/e2e_test.go:147** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2023-11-23T07:54:23Z

```diff
+var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Kueue visibility server", func() {
+	const defaultFlavor = "default-flavor"
+	var (
+		defaultRF    *kueue.ResourceFlavor
+		localQueue   *kueue.LocalQueue
+		clusterQueue *kueue.ClusterQueue
+		ns           *corev1.Namespace
+		sampleJob1   *batchv1.Job
+		sampleJob2   *batchv1.Job
+	)

+		}

+	})

+		gomega.Expect(util.DeleteNamespace(ctx, k8sClient, ns)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+	})

+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, defaultRF)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+
+			clusterQueue = testing.MakeClusterQueue("cluster-queue").
+				ResourceGroup(
+					*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas(defaultFlavor).
+						Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "1").
+						Obj(),
+				).
+				Preemption(kueue.ClusterQueuePreemption{
+					WithinClusterQueue: kueue.PreemptionPolicyLowerPriority,
+				}).
+				Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, clusterQueue)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+

+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, localQueue)).Should(gomega.Succeed())

+		})
+		ginkgo.AfterEach(func() {

+			gomega.Expect(util.DeleteAllJobsInNamespace(ctx, k8sClient, ns)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			util.ExpectClusterQueueToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, clusterQueue, true)
+			util.ExpectResourceFlavorToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, defaultRF, true)
+		})
+
+		ginkgo.It("Should fetch information about pending workloads", func() {
+			ginkgo.By("Have zero pending workloads", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func() int {
+					info, err := visibilityClient.ClusterQueues().GetPendingWorkloadsSummary(ctx, clusterQueue.Name, metav1.GetOptions{})
+					gomega.Expect(err).NotTo(gomega.HaveOccurred())
+					return len(info.Items)
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Equal(0))
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("Schedule two max capacity jobs", func() {
+				highPriorityClass := testing.MakePriorityClass("high").PriorityValue(100).Obj()

+				})

+				})

+					Queue(localQueue.Name).
+					Image("gcr.io/k8s-staging-perf-tests/sleep:v0.0.3", []string{"60s", "-termination-grace-period", "0s"}).

+					Image("gcr.io/k8s-staging-perf-tests/sleep:v0.0.3", []string{"1ms"}).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "1").

+					return int(*createdJob.Status.Ready)
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Equal(1))
+				// Make sure that pod can receive SIGTERM
+				time.Sleep(time.Second * 1)
```

  To update the thread, we go with the approach of terminating the job1 one from the test code. In order to make the test not flake we also set `backoffLimit=0` and `terminationGracePeriodSeconds=1`. The job can either fail or succeed, but it is not relevant for the test, because we just want to unblock capacity.
